# Longest Consecutive

```java
for(int a:nums) numsSet.add(a);

        int max = 1;

        for(int a: nums){
            int currMax = 1;
            boolean exist = true; // consecutive exist

            int i = 1;
            while(exist){
                if(numsSet.contains(a+i)){
                    currMax++;
                    i++;
                }else{
                    exist = false;
                    i = 1;
                }
            }
            max = Math.max(currMax, max);
        }
        return max;
    }
```
